    var itemsarray = [];
    var wisharray = [];

        function addToCompare(id) {
        var list = new cookieList("compareList");
        itemsarray=list.items();
        if(itemsarray=="null") {
           list.remove("null");
        } else if(itemsarray.length>=3) {
            return false;
        }
        productId=id.toString();
        var inArray = $.inArray(productId, itemsarray);
        if(inArray < 0){
            	list.add(productId);
                var count=list.items().length;
        $("#compare_property").html("("+count+")");
        $('#compare_list').append('<input type="hidden" name="property_list[]" value="'+productId+'">');
           	} else {
                return false;
   	}
        //alert(list.items());
      }
      
      function removeCompare(id) {
        var list = new cookieList("compareList");
        itemsarray=list.items();
        if(itemsarray=="null") {
           list.remove("null");
        }
        productId=id.toString();
        var inArray = $.inArray(productId, itemsarray);
        if(inArray != -1){
            	list.remove(productId);
                var count=list.items().length;
        $("#compare_property").html("("+count+")");
           	} else {
                return false;
   	}
        //alert(list.items());
      }
      
      function addToShortList(id) {
      var wish = new cookieList("shortList");
      wisharray=wish.items();
      if(wisharray=="null") {
           wish.remove("null");
        } else if(wisharray.length>=20) {
            return false;
        }
        wishId=id.toString();
        var inArray = $.inArray(wishId, wisharray);
        if(inArray < 0){
  		wish.add(wishId);
                var count=wish.items().length;
               $("#shortlist_property").html("["+count+"]");
        $('#short_list').append('<input type="hidden" name="property_list[]" value="'+wishId+'">');
           	} else {
                return false;
   	}
    }

    function addToSearchedList(id) {
    var search = new cookieList("searchList");
        itemsarray=search.items();
        if(itemsarray=="null") {
           search.remove("null");
        } else if(itemsarray.length>=10) {
            return false;
        }
        productId=id.toString();
        var inArray = $.inArray(productId, itemsarray);
        if(inArray < 0){
            var count=search.items().length;
            	search.add(productId);
                $("#searchlist_property").html("["+count+"]");
        $('#search_list').append('<input type="hidden" name="property_list[]" value="'+productId+'">');
          	} else {
                return false;
   	}
    }
    
    var cookieList = function(cookieName) {

    var cookie = $.cookie(cookieName);
    var items = cookie ? cookie.split(/,/) : new Array();

    return {
        "add": function(val) {
            items.push(val);
            $.cookie(cookieName, items.join(','), { path:'/' });
        },
        "remove": function(val) {
            indx = items.indexOf(val);
            if (indx != -1)
                items.splice(indx, 1);
            $.cookie(cookieName, items.join(','));
        },
        "clear": function() {
            items = '';
            $.cookie(cookieName, '', { path:'/'});
        },
        "items": function() {
            return items;
        }
    }
};
 function countCompareList() {
     var list = new cookieList("compareList");
     var total=list.items().length;
     $("#compare_property").html("("+total+")");
     array=list.items();
     for(var i=0; i<array.length; i++) {
         $('#compare_list').append('<input type="hidden" name="property_list[]" value="'+array[i]+'">');
     }
 }
 
 function countShortList() {
     var wish = new cookieList("shortList");
     var total=wish.items().length;
     $("#shortlist_property").html("["+total+"]");
     array=wish.items();
     for(var i=0; i<array.length; i++) {
         $('#short_list').append('<input type="hidden" name="property_list[]" value="'+array[i]+'">');
     }
 }

function countContactList() {

     for(var i=0; i<array.length; i++) {
         $('#contact_list').append('<input type="hidden" name="property_list[]" value="'+array[i]+'">');
     }
 }

 }


 function formSubmit(e) {
 var list = new cookieList("compareList");
 if(list.items().length<2) {
 $('#no-comparelist-modal1').modal('show');
     e.preventDefault();
 } else if (list.items().length>3) {
     $('#no-comparelist-modal2').modal('show');
  e.preventDefault();
  } else {
 $("#myForm").submit();
  }
    }

function formSubmitShortlist(e) {
 var wish = new cookieList("shortList");
 if(wish.items().length<=0) {
    $('#no-shortlist-modal').modal('show');
     e.preventDefault();
 } else {
 $("#shorList").submit();
  }
    }
    
    function formSubmitContactlist(e) {
 var contact = new cookieList("contactList");
 if(contact.items().length<=0) {

     e.preventDefault();
 } else {
 $("#contactList").submit();
  }
    }

 $("#searchList").submit();
  }
    }
    
    function saveCompareList(array,id) {
        var url="http://www.propertynepal.com/save-compare-listing";
        $.ajax({
        type:"GET",
        url:url,
        data:{list:array,uid:id},
        success: function(response){
            //console.log(response);
            },
        error: function(error) {
            console.log(error);
            }
    });
    }

    function countLoginList(userid) {
        var url="http://www.propertynepal.com/get-dashboard-count";
        $.ajax({
        type:"GET",
        url:url,
        data:{user_id:userid},
        success: function(count){
            for(var i=0; i<count.length; i++) {
            $("#count_"+i).html("["+count[i]+"]");
        }
            },
        error: function(error) {
                console.log(error);
            }
    });
    }
    
    function checkUserPropertyCountFront(uid) {
            var url="http://www.propertynepal.com/get-user-property-count";
            var redirectUrl="http://www.propertynepal.com/add-property";
            var dashboardUrl="http://www.propertynepal.com/myDashboard"+"/"+uid;
            $.ajax({
        type:"get",
        url:url,
        async:false,
        data:{userid:uid},
        success: function(response){
//            console.log(response);
            var status = response.trim();
            if(status=="Allowed") {
                location.href=redirectUrl;
            } else {
                location.href=dashboardUrl+"?display=true";
              }
            },
        error: function(error) {
            console.log(error);
            },
    });
        }

                                        <script>
function showAllPropertyType() {
    $(".ptype").show();
    $(".multiselect-all").show();
    $('.ptype input:checkbox').prop('checked', true);
    $('.ptype option').prop('selected', true);
    $(".multiselect-selected-text").html("All Selected");
}
function showCommercialPropertyType() {
    $(".ptype").hide();
    $(".multiselect-all").hide();
    $(".Commercial").show();
    $(".multiselect-selected-text").html("Commercial");
}
function setCommercialValues() {
    $('.ptype input:checkbox').prop('checked', false);
    $('.Commercial input:checkbox').prop('checked', true);
    $('.ptype option').prop('selected', false);
    $('.Commercial option').prop('selected', true);
}
$("#property_for").change(function () {
    if ($(this).val() == "commercial") {
        $("#property_for_2").show();
        showCommercialPropertyType();
        setCommercialValues();
    } else {
        $("#property_for_2").hide();
        showAllPropertyType();
    }
});
                                        </script>

                                    <script>
                                        function mapSearch() {
//                                            if(formValidation()){
                                            $("#hidden_keyword").val($("#hidden_keyword").val() + "," + $("#form_search").val());
                                            var serializeData = $("#form_data").serialize();
//                                                console.log(serializeData);
                                            location.href = "http://www.propertynepal.com/map-search" + "?" + serializeData;
//                                            }
                                        }
                                        function addKeyword(keyword) {
                                            selected_keywords.push(keyword);
                                            setKeywords();
                                        }
                                        function removeKeyword(n) {
                                            selected_keywords.splice(selected_keywords.indexOf(n), 1);
                                            setKeywords();
                                        }
                                        function setKeywords() {
                                            var text = "";
                                            selected_keywords.forEach(value => {
                                                text += '<span class="btn search-item-style">' + value + '<span class="badge"><i onclick="removeKeyword(\'' + value + '\')" class="fa fa-times"></i></span></span>';
                                            });
                                            $(".keywords").html(text);
                                            $("#form_search").val("");
                                            $("#hidden_keyword").val(selected_keywords.toString());

                                        }
                                        function showMinimumKeywords() {
                                            var text = "";
                                            if (selected_keywords.length >= 1) {
                                                text += '<span class="btn search-item-style">' + selected_keywords[0] + '<span class="badge"><i onclick="removeKeyword(\'' + selected_keywords[0] + '\')" class="fa fa-times"></i></span></span>';
                                            }
                                            if (selected_keywords.length >= 2) {
                                                $("#keyword_count").html('<span onclick="showAllKeywords()" class="btn search-item-style">+' + (selected_keywords.length - 1) + '</span>');
                                            }
                                            $(".keywords").html(text);
                                            $("#keyword_count").show();
                                        }
                                        function showAllKeywords() {
                                            $("#keyword_count").hide();
                                            var text = "";
                                            selected_keywords.forEach(value => {
                                                text += '<span class="btn search-item-style">' + value + '<span class="badge"><i onclick="removeKeyword(\'' + value + '\')" class="fa fa-times"></i></span></span>';
                                            });
                                            $(".keywords").html(text);
                                            //                            $("#form_search").val("");
                                            $("#hidden_keyword").val(selected_keywords.toString());
                                        }
                                    </script>

<script>
    $('.jcarousel')
            .on('jcarousel:create jcarousel:reload', function () {
                var element = $(this),
                        width = element.innerWidth();

                if (width > 900) {
                    width = width / 1;
                } else if (width > 600) {
                    width = width / 1;
                }

                element.jcarousel('items').css('width', width + 'px');
            })
            .jcarousel({
                // Your configurations options
            });
</script>

<script>
    $('.togglefilter').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var notthis = $('.active').not(this);
        notthis.find('.icon-minus').addClass('icon-plus').removeClass('icon-minus');
        notthis.toggleClass('active').next('.filter-data-cont').slideToggle(3000);
        $(this).toggleClass('active').next().slideToggle("fast");
        $(this).children('i').toggleClass('icon-plus icon-minus');
    });
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">
    var selected_keywords = "State 3";
        selected_keywords = selected_keywords.split(',');
    $(document).ready(function () {
        // initialize at the begining
        showAllKeywords();
        $('body').click(function (evt) {
            //For descendants of menu_content being clicked, remove this check if you do not want to put constraint on descendants.
            if ($(evt.target).closest('#form_container').length) {
                return;
            } else {
                //           hideAll();
                showMinimumKeywords();
            }

        });
        $('#listing-filter-prop-typ, #room').multiselect({
            enableClickableOptGroups: true,
            includeSelectAllOption: true
        });
        
        $('#room').multiselect({
            enableClickableOptGroups: true,
            includeSelectAllOption: true
        });
        // scripts for autocomplete
        $.get("http://www.propertynepal.com/api/location/get-property-locations", function (data, status) {
            console.log(data);
            var availableLocations = data.data;
            $("#form_search").autocomplete({
                //            source: availableLocations,
                source: function (request, response) {
                    if ($("#form_search").val().length >= 3) {
                        $.ajax({
                            url: "http://www.propertynepal.com/api/location/get-property-locations?keyword=" + $("#form_search").val(),
                            dataType: "json",
                            data: {
                                q: request.term
                            },
                            success: function (data) {
                                $("#location_laoding").hide();
                                response(data.data);
                            }
                        });
                    }
                },
                delay: 500,
                select: function (event, ui) {
                    var keyword = ui.item.label;
                    keyword = keyword.indexOf(',') == -1 ? keyword : keyword.substr(0, keyword.indexOf(','));
                    addKeyword(keyword);
                    $("#form_search").attr("placeholder", "Location or Keyword");
                    $("#form_search").removeClass("custom_error");
                    return false;
                },
            });
        });
    });
</script>

<script>



    function contactForm(id) {
        $("#contact_detail_" + id).fancybox({
            'onStart': function () {
                $("#contact_form_" + id).css("display", "block");
            },
            'onClosed': function () {
                $("#contact_form_" + id).css("display", "none");
            },
            //'modal':true,
            'closeBtn': true

        });
    }

    function reportForm(id) {
        $("#report_detail_" + id).fancybox({
            'onStart': function () {
                $("#report_form_" + id).css("display", "block");
            },
            'onClosed': function () {
                $("#report_form_" + id).css("display", "none");
            },
            //'modal':true,
            'closeBtn': true

        });
    }
    function goToDetailPage(id, cursor) {
        if (cursor == "") {
            window.open('http://www.propertynepal.com/propertydetail' + '/' + id, "_blank");
        } else {
            return false;
        }
    }

    function goToHome() {
        window.location.href = "http://www.propertynepal.com";
    }

    function formValidation() {
        var return_status = true;
        if ($("#hidden_keyword").val() == "" && $("#form_search").val() == "") {
            $("#form_search").attr("placeholder", "Search cannot be empty");
            $("#form_search").addClass("custom_error");
            return_status = false;
        } else {
            $("#form_search").removeClass("custom_error");
        }
//        if ($("#min_price").val() != "") {
//            if ($("#min_price").val() >= $("#max_price").val()) {
//                $("#min_price").addClass("custom_error");
//                $("#max_price").addClass("custom_error");
//                return_status = false;
//            }
//        } else {
//            $("#min_price").removeClass("custom_error");
//            $("#max_price").removeClass("custom_error");
//        }

if($('.multi_rooms input:checkbox').is(':checked')) {
        $("#rooms_err_msg").hide();
        } else {
            $("#rooms_err_msg").show();
            return_status= false;
        }
        
if(validateBudget()==true) {
        $("#min_price_unit").removeClass("custom_error");
                $("#max_price_unit").removeClass("custom_error");
    } else {
        $("#min_price_unit").addClass("custom_error");
                $("#max_price_unit").addClass("custom_error");
        return_status= false;
    }
        if ($("#min_area").val() != "") {
            if ($("#min_area").val() >= $("#max_area").val()) {
                $("#min_area").addClass("custom_error");
                $("#max_area").addClass("custom_error");
                return_status = false;
            }
        } else {
            $("#min_area").removeClass("custom_error");
            $("#max_area").removeClass("custom_error");
        }
        if ($('.ptype input:checkbox').is(':checked')) {
            $(".multiselect-selected-text").removeClass("custom_error");
        } else {
            $(".multiselect-selected-text").addClass("custom_error");
            return_status = false;
        }
       return return_status;
    }

function validateBudget() {
        var min_price=$("#min_price").val();
        var min_price_unit=$("#min_price_unit").val();
        var max_price=$("#max_price").val();
        var max_price_unit=$("#max_price_unit").val();
        var allowed_unit=[];
        switch(min_price_unit) {
            case "thousand":
                allowed_units = ["thousand", "lakh", "crore"];
                if(jQuery.inArray(max_price_unit, allowed_units) != -1) {
                    $("#min_price_unit").css("border", "");
                    $("#max_price_unit").css("border", "");
                    if(max_price>min_price) {
                    $("#min_price").css("border", "");
                    $("#max_price").css("border", "");
                    return true;
                    break;
                } else {
                    $("#min_price").css("border", "1px solid red");
                    $("#max_price").css("border", "1px solid red");
                    return false;
                    break;
                }
                } else {
                    $("#min_price_unit").css("border", "1px solid red");
                    $("#max_price_unit").css("border", "1px solid red");
                    return false;
                    break;
                }
        case "lakh":
                allowed_units = ["lakh", "crore"];
                if(jQuery.inArray(max_price_unit, allowed_units) != -1) {
                    $("#min_price_unit").css("border", "");
                    $("#max_price_unit").css("border", "");
                    if(max_price>min_price) {
                    $("#min_price").css("border", "");
                    $("#max_price").css("border", "");
                    return true;
                    break;
                } else {
                    $("#min_price").css("border", "1px solid red");
                    $("#max_price").css("border", "1px solid red");
                    return false;
                    break;
                }
            } else {
                $("#min_price_unit").css("border", "1px solid red");
                $("#max_price_unit").css("border", "1px solid red");
                    return false;
                    break;
            }
        case "crore":
            allowed_units = ["crore"];
            if(jQuery.inArray(max_price_unit, allowed_units) != -1) {
                $("#min_price_unit").css("border", "");
                $("#max_price_unit").css("border", "");
                if(max_price>min_price) {
                $("#min_price").css("border", "");
                $("#max_price").css("border", "");
                    return true;
                    break;
                } else {
                    $("#min_price").css("border", "1px solid red");
                    $("#max_price").css("border", "1px solid red");
                    return false;
                    break;
                }
            } else {
                $("#min_price_unit").css("border", "1px solid red");
                $("#max_price_unit").css("border", "1px solid red");
                    return false;
                    break;
            }
        }
    }
    
    $("#form_data").submit(function () {
        var returnValue = formValidation();
        if (returnValue) {
            var property_type = $("#property_type").val();
            if (property_type == "dealer") {
                location.href = "http://www.propertynepal.com/agents" + "?keyword=" + $("#hidden_keyword").val() + "," + $("#form_search").val();
                return false;
            }
        }
        return returnValue;
        $("#hidden_keyword").val($("#hidden_keyword").val() + "," + $("#form_search").val());
        $(this).append(newFormField);
        return true;
    });
</script>
